  - **B1 (caught by the verifier, my journal framing was wrong):** the reseller shell did NOT bundle ‚Äî `expo export` failed on `node:crypto` because App/i18n runtime-imported the `@platform/contracts`/`@platform/i18n` barrels, whose node-only modules (drift-check CLI, copy-lint loader) Metro cannot resolve. My earlier entry framed the gap as "no emulator available" ‚Äî the truth was catchable without any emulator, and the verifier caught it. **Fixed:** the RN bundle imports no node-only barrel (type-only catalog import; card values from a checked-in snapshot that a vitest test pins to the pinned `computeWaterfall` ¬ß5.4 baseline; contracts/i18n/commerce-core are devDependencies; a test bans runtime barrel imports in shell code). **Proof: `expo export --platform android` now produces the 1.77 MB Hermes bundle** (`_evidence/expo-export-bundle.txt`). The PWA shell boot was already proven in real Chromium (Playwright 2/2).

## 2026-07-11 ¬∑ CI INCIDENT #3 (expo-preview red on its first armed runs) ¬∑ fixed on main `21400d0`
- **Both armed `expo-preview` runs were red** (this repo √ó2; boutik √ó4, sera √ó2 ‚Äî one shared defect). Diagnosis from the complete Actions logs (pulled via API, log-copied): token check, checkout, install, `eas init --non-interactive --force` (`‚úî Project successfully linked (ID: 3436dab2-922f-4f80-beeb-e17e85f1f099)`) and `update:configure` (`‚úî Configured updates.url`) all PASSED ‚Äî the failure is the third command's bundling: `SyntaxError: index.ts: Cannot find module 'babel-preset-expo'`, identical across the three repos. The token and the founder's account are NOT the cause.
- **Root cause (config-class, reproduced in boutik's cold clone, byte-identical error):** `babel.config.js` names `babel-preset-expo`; the app manifest never declared it; pnpm strict isolation leaves it unresolvable from the app directory on a fresh install; babel has no fallback (direct `@babel/core` transform emulation).
- **Why WO-4.0's evidence missed it (failure-mode #8, named):** the `expo start --offline` boot probe transforms nothing until a client connects, and local exports silently reused Metro's cross-directory content-hash cache (`$TMPDIR/metro-cache`), bypassing babel. Standing lesson: bundling evidence = a cache-isolated `expo export`, never a dev-server boot line.
- **Fix `21400d0`:** `babel-preset-expo ~13.2.5` (expo 53.0.27's own declared range) added to `apps/reseller-app` devDependencies; lockfile by regeneration (+3 lines, zero new packages, dup-key assert 0). Evidence: resolve-from-app-dir OK ¬∑ gates exit 0 (ALL GATES GREEN) ¬∑ cache-isolated export exit 0 (579 modules bundled) ¬∑ boutik cold-clone proof of the identical fix passed.
- **The founder's next expo-preview runs are the only closure** ‚Äî this entry claims the local reproduction and fix, never the publish.

Toolchain fontTools 4.63.0 + brotli. OFL 1.1 texts committed both surfaces.
- **THE MONEY-RENDER / cmap GUARD ‚Äî a REAL find, not ceremony:** the guard derives its required charset from (a) the REAL formatter (`formatFcfa`/`FCFA`, consumed untouched) and (b) the app's OWN `i18n/catalog.json` (grounded, not hand-typed). It caught **two** gaps: ‚ëÝ **U+202F** (the narrow no-break space fr-FR emits between franc thousands, ¬´ 11 500 F ¬ª) ‚Äî Bricolage carries it natively, **Instrument Sans does not**; consciously **mapped U+202F ‚Üí the font's space advance in the cmap** of every lacking face (a deliberate cmap pin, recorded in `FASO-PREMIUM-BUILD.md` ‚Äî closes the honest gap Archivo left open, no tofu, no fallback swap). ‚ë° **U+2212** (the typographic MINUS in the reseller fee line ¬´ Part Shop+ (20 %) : ‚àí {amount} ¬ª) ‚Äî was outside the first charset; **added to the subset and rebuilt**. Both now covered by every face; `formatter-emits-what-font-lacks = STOP` is enforced mechanically (the guard fails LOUD on any uncovered emitted codepoint).
- **THE GUARD IS SHA-BOUND, NOT TRUSTING:** `faso-premium.coverage.json` per surface carries each shipped file's sha256 + its real cmap coverage (read by fontTools from the bytes). `test/faso-fonts.test.ts` (both surfaces, 6 tests each) re-hashes every committed file and refuses a manifest that does not describe the bytes on disk; checks the flavour magic (sfnt 0x00010000 / woff2 'wOF2'); asserts every money-formatter codepoint + every catalog non-ASCII codepoint is covered by all four faces; and asserts the four-and-only-four face set (no stray 500/600).
- **PWA PAYLOAD BUDGET (established BEFORE any view is styled ‚Äî the tightest gate):** four woff2 = **84 228 B = 82.3 KB** (Bricolage-Bold 22 968 ¬∑ Bricolage-ExtraBold 22 364 ¬∑ Instrument-Regular 19 244 ¬∑ Instrument-Bold 19 652). **217.7 KB under** the 300 KB gate. Transition peak with Archivo still present = 114 580 B (111.9 KB) ‚Äî still 188 KB under; Archivo retires in WO-FP-PWA. Documented in `apps/buyer-pwa/public/fonts/FASO-PREMIUM-BUDGET.md`; the PWA guard asserts the total `< 300*1024`.
- **RN EMBED (repo idiom, DATA ONLY):** `apps/reseller-app/src/ui/faso-fonts.ts` mirrors `fonts.ts` exactly ‚Äî `DISPLAY_FAMILY`/`TEXT_FAMILY` (the canon token's names), `DISPLAY_WEIGHTS`/`TEXT_WEIGHTS` (weight‚Üíttf), `FONT_FALLBACK='System'`. ### 2026-07-18 ¬∑ addendum ‚Äî CI cold-clone root cause (lockfile `resolution.repo` scheme-strip)
- **Branch ci #58/#59 failed at `pnpm install --frozen-lockfile`** (not a gate): `git clone github.com/beurni2/platform-contracts.git ‚Ä¶ does not exist` ‚Äî a SCHEME-LESS clone URL. Cache MISS (new lockfile hash from the re-pin) forced a cold clone that exposed it; main/sera stay green because the pnpm store is cached on the old hash.
- **False lead (#59):** added a 4th CI insteadOf for the scheme-less form ‚Äî still failed. pnpm's git fetcher does NOT take the clone URL from git insteadOf; it reads it from the lockfile's `resolution.repo` field.
- **ROOT CAUSE:** my lockfile was resolved in THIS sandbox, whose git config rewrites `https://github.com/` ‚Üí the local proxy; pnpm wrote `resolution.repo: github.com/beurni2/platform-contracts.git` ‚Äî **scheme-stripped**. My `git@`‚Üí`github.com/` normalization never touched it (no `git@` there). sera's working lockfile carries `repo: https://github.com/‚Ä¶`.
- **FIX:** restored the `https://` scheme on all 5 `resolution.repo` fields (certification, contracts, i18n, kernel-types, ui-tokens) so the lockfile byte-matches sera's proven cold-clone form; reverted the dead #59 ci.yml rule. Committed lockfile stays gate-clean (0 `git@`, lockfile-url-form green). Re-dispatching ci for the authoritative proof.
- **CI GREEN (authoritative):** branch `ci` run #60 @ `b53571f` ‚Äî **success**, full suite (install ‚Üí build ‚Üí playwright 43/43 ‚Üí every invariant gate, positives + negatives). Cold-clone now works (the repo-scheme fix); this run was a cache MISS that cloned and passed, proving the fix. Founder approved merge.
